<div><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 8.7pt; margin-left: 218.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">说明</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.7pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 13pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-right: 5.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">本合同文本为示范文本，由中华人民共和国住房和城乡建设部、中华人民共和国国家工商行政管理总局共同制定。各地可在有关法律法规、规定的范围内，结合实际情况调整合同相应内容。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 5.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">签订本合同前，出卖人应当向买受人出示《商品房预售许可证》及其他有关证书和证明文件。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 5.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">3.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">出卖人应当就合同重大事项对买受人尽到提示义务。买受人应当审慎签订合同，在签订本合同前，要仔细阅读合同条款，特别是审阅其中具有选择性、补充性、修改性的内容，注意防范潜在的市场风险和交易风险。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 5.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">4.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">本合同文本【】中选择内容、空格部位填写内容及其他需要删除或添加的内容，双方当</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.7pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">事人应当协商确定。【】中选择内容，以划 √ 方式选定；对于实际情况未发生或双方当事人不</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.45pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">作约定时，应当在空格部位打× ，以示删除。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 5.5pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">5.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">出卖人与买受人可以针对本合同文本中没有约定或者约定不明确的内容，根据所售项目</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">的具体情况在相关条款后的空白行中进行补充约定，也可以另行签订补充协议。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 5.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">6.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">双方当事人可以根据实际情况决定本合同原件的份数，并在签订合同时认真核对，以确</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.3pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">保各份合同内容一致；在任何情况下，出卖人和买受人都应当至少持有一份合同原件。</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65545;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.004.png" width="19" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; margin-left: 447.41pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p></div></div>  
<div><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 8.7pt; margin-left: 190.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">专业术语解释</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.7pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 13pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-right: 10.55pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">商品房预售：是指房地产开发企业将正在建设中的取得《商品房预售许可证》的商品房预先出售给买受人，并由买受人支付定金或房价款的行为。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">法定代理人：是指依照法律规定直接取得代理权的人。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.45pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">3.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">套内建筑面积：是指成套房屋的套内建筑面积，由套内使用面积、套内墙体面积、套内阳台建筑面积三部分组成。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-right: 5.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">4.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">房屋的建筑面积：是指房屋外墙</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（柱</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.55pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">勒脚以上各层的外围水平投影面积，包括阳台、挑廊、地下室、室外楼梯等，且具备有上盖，结构牢固，层高 </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.20M</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> 以上</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.3pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">含 </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.20M）的永久性建筑。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">5.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">不可抗力：是指不能预见、不能避免并不能克服的客观情况。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 5.2pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">6.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">民用建筑节能：是指在保证民用建筑使用功能和室内热环境质量的前提下，降低其使用</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">过程中能源消耗的活动。民用建筑是指居住建筑、国家机关办公建筑和商业、服务业、教育、卫生等其他公共建筑。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">7.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">房屋登记：是指房屋登记机构依法将房屋权利和其他应当记载的事项在房屋登记簿上予以记载的行为。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">8.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">所有权转移登记：是指商品房所有权从出卖人转移至买受人所办理的登记类型。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.45pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">9.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">房屋登记机构：是指直辖市、市、县人民政府建设</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（房地产）主管部门或者其设置的负责房屋登记工作的机构。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">10.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">分割拆零销售：是指房地产开发企业将成套的商品住宅分割为数部分分别出售给买受人的销售方式。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 44.2pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -16.35pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">11.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">返本销售：是指房地产开发企业以定期向买受人返还购房款的方式销售商品房的行为。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">12.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">售后包租：是指房地产开发企业以在一定期限内承租或者代为出租买受人所购该企业商品房的方式销售商品房的行为。</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65545;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.005.png" width="19" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; margin-left: 447.41pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p></div></div>  
<div><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 8.7pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center; font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">商品房买卖合同</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.4pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center; font-size: 14pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（预 售）</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.55pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 16.5pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-right: 5.65pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">出卖人向买受人出售其开发建设的房屋，双方当事人应当在自愿、平等、公平及诚实信</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">用的基础上，根据《中华人民共和国合同法》、《中华人民共和国物权法》、《中华人民共和国城市房地产管理法》等法律、法规的规定，就商品房买卖相关内容协商达成一致意见，签订本商品房</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买卖合同。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 9.1pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第一章</span><span style="width: 19.95pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">合同当事人</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 9pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; <div><p style="margin-top: 1.2pt; margin-right: 7.8pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。抵押权人同意该商品房转让的证明及关于抵押的相关约定见附件三。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.95pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">出卖人对该商品房享有合法权利；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房没有出售给除本合同买受人以外的其他人；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房没有司法查封或其他限制转让的情况；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">4.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-right: 5.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">5.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 415.05pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。如该商品房权利状况与上述情况不符，导致不能完成本合同登记备案或房屋所有</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 7.8pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">权转移登记的，买受人有权解除合同。买受人解除合同的，应当书面通知出卖人。出卖人</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">应当自解除合同通知送达之日</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">起</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">15</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> 日内退还买受人已付全部房</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">款</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（含已付贷款部分</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，并自</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买受人付款之日起，按照</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">%（不低于中国人民银行公布的同期贷款基准利率）计算给付 利息。给买受人造成损失的，由出卖人支付【已付房价款一倍</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">】</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">【买受人全部损失】的赔偿金。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 9.1pt; margin-right: 4.9pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">计价方式与价款</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">出卖人与买受人按照下列第</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">种方式计算该商品房价款：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.65pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 94.11pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">币种</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">元，总价款 为</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 7.16pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">币种</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">元（大写</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; letter-spacing: -4.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 9.9pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; letter-spacing: 0.75pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，总价款 </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">为</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 9.31pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">币种</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">元（大写</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">3.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">按照套计算，该商品房总价款为</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 72.61pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">币种</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="width: 48.28pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">元（大写</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 106.03pt; text-indent: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 85.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">计算，该商品房总价款为</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 84.63pt; text-indent: 0pt; <div><p style="margin-top: 1.2pt; margin-left: 27.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（一</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，账号为</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.05pt; margin-right: 13.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该比率不 </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">低于第（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.3pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.45pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">项中的比率</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">的违约金。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.05pt; margin-right: 13.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">本条所称逾期应付款是指依照第七条及附件四约定的到期应付款与该期实际已付款的差额；采取分期付款的，按照相应的分期应付款与该期的实际已付款的差额确定。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 41.05pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -8.2pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -4.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 415.05pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65545;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.009.png" width="19" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; margin-left: 447.41pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p></div></div>  
<div><p style="margin-top: 0.5pt; margin-right: 4.9pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第四章</span><span style="width: 19.95pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">商品房交付条件与交付手续</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.65pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 8.5pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.05pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第九条</span><span style="width: 18.33pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">商品房交付条件</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房交付时应当符合下列第</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1、2</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">、</span><span style="width: 88.5pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">、</span><span style="width: 51.94pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">项所列条件：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房已取得建设工程竣工验收备案证明文件；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房已取得房屋测绘报告；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">3.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 415.05pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 5.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">4.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 415.05pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房为住宅的，出卖人还需提供《住宅使用说明书》和《住宅质量保证书》。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.95pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第十条</span><span style="width: 18.33pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">商品房相关设施设备交付条件</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（一</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">基础设施设备</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.45pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">供水、排水：交付时供水、排水配套设施齐全，并与城市公共供水、排水管网连接。使用自建设施供水的，供水的水质符合国家规定的饮用水卫生标准，</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 423.3pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">供电：交付时纳入城市供电网络并正式供电，</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 423.3pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-right: 5.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">3.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">供暖</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.6pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">：</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">交付时供热系统符合供热配建标准，使用城市集中供热的，纳入城市集中供热管 网</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，</span><span style="width: 72.8pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">4.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">燃气：交付时完成室内燃气管道的敷设，并与城市燃气管网连接，保证燃气供应，</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 423.3pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">5.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">电话通信：交付时线路敷设到户；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">6.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">有线电视：交付时线路敷设到户；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">7.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">宽带网络：交付时线路敷设到户。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">以上第 1、2、3 项由出卖人负责办理开通手续并承担相关费用；第 4、5、6、7 项需要买受人自行办理开通手续。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-right: 10.65pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">如果在约定期限内基础设施设备未达到交付使用条件，双方同意按照下列第</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 124.3pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">种方式处理：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（ 1）以上设施中第 1、2、3、4 项在约定交付日未达到交付条件的，出卖人按照本合同第十二条的约定承担逾期交付责任。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.75pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">5</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.75pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">项未按时达到交付使用条件的，出卖人按日向买受人支付</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 119.99pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">元的违约金</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.6pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.45pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: -0.05pt; text-align: center; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">6</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">项未按时达到交付使用条件</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，出卖人按日向买受人支</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">付</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 89.65pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 29.8pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">元的违约</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">金</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">7</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">项未按时达到交付使用条件</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">元的违</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">约</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。以上设施未达到上述条件的，双方同意按照以下方式处理：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: justify; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">小区内绿地率未达到上述约定条件的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，</span><span style="width: 272.35pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: justify; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">小区内非市政道路未达到上述约定条件的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，</span><span style="width: 255.23pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: justify; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">3.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">规划的车位、车库未达到上述约定条件的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，</span><span style="width: 255.23pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: justify; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">4.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">物业服务用房未达到上述约定条件的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，</span><span style="width: 272.35pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-right: 5.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">5.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">其他设施未达到上述约定条件的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，</span><span style="width: 289.46pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。关于本项目内相关设施设备的具体约定见附件五。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.95pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第十一条</span><span style="width: 20.78pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">交付时间和手续</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（一）出卖人应当在</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 47.74pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">年</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 24.69pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">月</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 24.69pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日前向买受人交付该商品房。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（二）该商品房达到第九条、第十条约定的交付条件后，出卖人应当在交付日期届满前</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.65pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 30.25pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">不少于 </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">10</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> 日</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">将查验房屋的时间、办理交付手续的时间地点以及应当携带的证件</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">材料的通知书面送达买受人。买受人未收到交付通知书的，以本合同约定的交付日期届满之日为办理交付手续的时间，以该商品房所在地为办理交付手续的地点。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 5.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 423.3pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。交付该商品房时，出卖人应当出示满足第九条约定的证明文件。出卖人不出示证明文件或</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 10.8pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">者出示的证明文件不齐全，不能满足第九条约定条件的，买受人有权拒绝接收，由此产生的逾期交付责任由出卖人承担，并按照第十二条处理。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（三</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">查验房屋</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">办理交付手续前，买受人有权对该商品房进行查验，出卖人不得以缴纳相关税费或者签</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65542;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.011.png" width="18" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; margin-left: 447.78pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p></div></div>  
<div><p style="margin-top: 1.2pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">署物业管理文件作为买受人查验和办理交付手续的前提条件。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.65pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买受人查验的该商品房存在下列除地基基础和主体结构外的其他质量问题的，由出卖人按照有关工程和产品质量规范、标准自查验次日起</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> 日内负责修复，并承 担修复费用，修复后再行交付。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（ 1）屋面、墙面、地面渗漏或开裂等；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（ 2）管道堵塞；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（ 3）门窗翘裂、五金件损坏；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（ 4）灯具、电器等电气设备不能正常使用；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">5</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="width: 406.19pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">6</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="width: 406.19pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-right: 10.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">3.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">查验该商品房后，双方应当签署商品房交接单。由于买受人原因导致该商品房未能按期交付的，双方同意按照以下方式处理：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="width: 406.19pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="width: 406.19pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.15pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第十二条</span><span style="width: 20.78pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">逾期交付责任</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">除不可抗力外，出卖人未按照第十一条约定的时间将该商品房交付买受人的，双方同意按照下列第</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 33.49pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">种方式处理：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -4.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">按照逾期时间，分别处理</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.6pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1）和（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.6pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2）不作累加</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -4.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-right: 10.2pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1）逾期在</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 73.72pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日之</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">内</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（该期限应当不多于第八</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.6pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">条</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.9pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.6pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）项中的期限</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第十一条约定的交付期限届满之次日起至实际交付之日</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.3pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">止</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，出卖人按日计算向买受人支付</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">全部房价款万分</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">之</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; letter-spacing: 0.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; letter-spacing: 0.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; letter-spacing: 0.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">的违约</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.3pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">金</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（该违约金比率应当不低于第八条</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 1.3pt; letter-spacing: 0.75pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（该期限应当与本条</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.3pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">项中的期限相同）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">后</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.75pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，买受人</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。买受人解除合同</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.6pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，应当书面通知出卖</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">人</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.6pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。出卖人应当自解除合同通知送</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.3pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">达之日</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">起</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">15</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.3pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日内退还买受人已付全部房</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">款</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.3pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（含已付贷款部分</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.3pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，并自买受人付款之日</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">起</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.3pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，按</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">照</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">%（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">不低于中国人民银行公布的同期贷款基准利率）计算给付利</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">息</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.55pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">同</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">时</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，出卖人 </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">按照全部房价款的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">% 向买受人支付违约金。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 10.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买受人要求继续履行合同的，合同继续履行，出卖人按日计算向买受人支付全部房价款万分之</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 14.6pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该比率应当不低于本条第</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.6pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1）项中的比率）的违约金。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 36.05pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -8.2pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -4.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 415.05pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65542;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.012.png" width="18" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; <div><p style="margin-top: 0.5pt; margin-right: 4.9pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第五章</span><span style="width: 19.95pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">面积差异处理方式</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.65pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 8.5pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.05pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第十三条</span><span style="width: 20.78pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">面积差异处理</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.7pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房交付时，出卖人应当向买受人出示房屋测绘报告，并向买受人提供该商品房的面积实测数据（以下简称实测面积</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -4.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。实测面积与第三条载明的预测面积发生误差的，双方同意按照第</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">种方式处理。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: 17pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">根据第六条按照套内建筑面积计价的约定，双方同意按照下列原则处理：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（ 1）套内建筑面积误差比绝对值在 3% 以内（含 3%）的，据实结算房价款；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（ 2）套内建筑面积误差比绝对值超出 3% 时，买受人有权解除合同。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买受人解除合同</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，应当书面通知出卖</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">人</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。出卖人应当自解除合同通知送达之日</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">起</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.65pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">15</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.65pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日内退还买受人已付全部房</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.6pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">款</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（含已付贷款部分</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，并自买受人付款之日起，按</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">照</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.6pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">%</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">不低于中国人民银行公布的同期贷款基准利率）计算给付利息。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-right: 5.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买受人选择不解除合同的，实测套内建筑面积大于预测套内建筑面积时，套内建筑面积误差比在 3% 以内（含 3%）部分的房价款由买受人补足；超出 3% 部分的房价款由出卖人承担， 产权归买受人所有。实测套内建筑面积小于预测套内建筑面积时，套内建筑面积误差比绝对值在 3% 以内（含 3%）部分的房价款由出卖人返还买受人；绝对值超出 3% 部分的房价款由出卖人双倍返还买受人。</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65540;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.013.png" width="19" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; margin-left: 452.41pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p></div></div>
