<div><p style="margin-top: 0.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 7pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-left: 70.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -2;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.014.png" width="252" height="1" alt="" style="margin-top: 10.04pt; margin-left: 115.32pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">套内建筑面积误差比 =</span></p><br style="clear: both;"><p style="margin-top: 2.35pt; margin-left: 57.3pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -52.75pt; line-height: 111%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">实测套内建筑面积－预测套内建筑面积预测套内建筑面积</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.55pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><br style="clear: both;"></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-left: 5.9pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">×100%</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65540;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.015.png" width="19" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; margin-left: 452.41pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p></div></div>  
<div><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: 17pt; line-height: 15.25pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; font-size: 11pt; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; font-size: 11pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">根据第六条按照建筑面积计价的约定，双方同意按照下列原则处理：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 5.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（ </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">建筑面积、套内建筑面积误差比绝对值均在 3</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.7pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">% 以内</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（含 </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">3%）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">的，根据实测建筑面积结算房价款；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 0.95pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; text-indent: -5.5pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（ 2）建筑面积、套内建筑面积误差比绝对值其中有一项超出 3% 时，买受人有权解除合同。买受人解除合同的，应当书面通知出卖人。出卖人应当自解除合同通知送达之日起 15 日</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">内退还买受人已付全部房</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.6pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">款</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（含已付贷款部分</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，并自买受人付款之日起，按</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">照</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 120.73pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.6pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">%</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">不低于中国人民银行公布的同期贷款基准利率）计算给付利息。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 10.45pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买受人选择不解除合同的，实测建筑面积大于预测建筑面积时，建筑面积误差比在 3% 以内（含 3%）部分的房价款由买受人补足，超出 3% 部分的房价款由出卖人承担，产权归买受人所有。实测建筑面积小于预测建筑面积时，建筑面积误差比绝对值在 3% 以内（含 3%）部分的房价款由出卖人返还买受人；绝对值超出 3% 部分的房价款由出卖人双倍返还买受人。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 2.35pt; margin-left: 196pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 12.4pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; font-size: 11pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">实测建筑面积－预测建筑面积</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65540;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.016.png" width="19" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; margin-left: 452.41pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p></div></div>  
<div><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-left: 81.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 12.65pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -1;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.014.png" width="252" height="1" alt="" style="margin-top: 6.14pt; margin-left: 93.32pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; font-size: 11pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">建筑面积误差比 =</span></p><p style="margin-top: 6pt; margin-left: 68.3pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><br style="clear: both;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">预测建筑面积</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-right: 63.8pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 62.4pt; text-align: center; line-height: 14.35pt;"><br style="clear: both;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; font-size: 11pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">×100%</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65540;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.017.png" width="19" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; margin-left: 452.41pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p></div></div>  
<div><p style="margin-top: 0.1pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（ 3）因设计变更造成面积差异，双方不解除合同的，应当签署补充协议。</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65540;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.018.png" width="19" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; margin-left: 452.41pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p></div></div>  
<div><p style="margin-top: 1.2pt; margin-right: 10.15pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">3.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.3pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">根据第六条按照套计价的，出卖人承诺在房屋平面图中标明详细尺寸，并约定误差</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">范围。该商品房交付时，套型与设计图纸不一致或者相关尺寸超出约定的误差范围，双方约定如下：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 423.3pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 43.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">4.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">双方自行约定：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 423.3pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.5pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 8.5pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第六章</span><span style="width: 19.95pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">规划设计变更</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.65pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 8.5pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.05pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第十四条</span><span style="width: 20.78pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">规划变更</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.4pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（一）出卖人应当按照城乡规划主管部门核发的建设工程规划许可证规定的条件建设商品房，不得擅自变更。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">双方签订合同后，涉及该商品房规划用途、面积、容积率、绿地率、基础设施、公共服务及其他配套设施等规划许可内容经城乡规划主管部门批准变更的，出卖人应当在变更确立之日起</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">10 日内将书面通知送达买受人。出卖人未在规定期限内通知买受人的，买受人有权解除合同。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（二）买受人应当在通知送达之日起 15 日内做出是否解除合同的书面答复。买受人逾期未予以书面答复的，视同接受变更。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 27.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（三）买受人解除合同的，应当书面通知出卖人。出卖人应当自解除合同通知送达之日起</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">15</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日内退还买受人已付全部房</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">款</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（含已付贷款部分</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，并自买受人付款之日</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">起</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，按</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">照</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 119.88pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">%</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: -5.5pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（不低于中国人民银行公布的同期贷款基准利率</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">计算给付利息</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.75pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">同时，出卖人按照全部房价款的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 19.99pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">% 向买受人支付违约金。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买受人不解除合同的，有权要求出卖人赔偿由此造成的损失，双方约定如下：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 423.3pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.15pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第十五条</span><span style="width: 20.78pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">设计变更</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.5pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（一）双方签订合同后，出卖人按照法定程序变更建筑工程施工图设计文件，涉及下列可能影响买受人所购商品房质量或使用功能情形的，出卖人应当在变更确立之日起 10 日内将书面通知送达买受人。出卖人未在规定期限内通知买受人的，买受人有权解除合同。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 43.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房结构形式、户型、空间尺寸、朝向；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 43.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">供热、采暖方式；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">3.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 415.05pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">4.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 415.05pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">5.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 415.05pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65540;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.019.png" width="19" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; margin-left: 452.41pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p></div></div>  
<div><p style="margin-top: 1.2pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（二）买受人应当在通知送达之日起 15 日内做出是否解除合同的书面答复。买受人逾期未予以书面答复的，视同接受变更。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 27.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（三）买受人解除合同的，应当书面通知出卖人。出卖人应当自解除合同通知送达之日起</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">5 日内退还买受人已付全部房款（含已付贷款部分</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，并自买受人付款之日起</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">按照</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 119.88pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">%</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: -5.5pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（不低于中国人民银行公布的同期贷款基准利率</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">计算给付利息</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.75pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">同时，出卖人按照全部房价款的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 19.99pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">% 向买受人支付违约金。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买受人不解除合同的，有权要求出卖人赔偿由此造成的损失，双方约定如下：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 423.3pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.45pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 8.5pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.05pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第七章</span><span style="width: 19.95pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">商品房质量及保修责任</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.7pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 8.5pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第十六条</span><span style="width: 20.78pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">商品房质量</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 27.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（一</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">地基基础和主体结构</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">出卖人承诺该商品房地基基础和主体结构合格，并符合国家及行业标准。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">经检测不合格的，买受人有权解除合同。买受人解除合同的，应当书面通知出卖人。出卖</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">人应当自解除合同通知送达之日</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">起</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">15</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> 日内退还买受人已付全部房</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">款</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（含已付贷款部分</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，并</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">自买受人付款之日起，按照</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">%（不低于中国人民银行公布的同期贷款基准利率）计算给 </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">付利</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">息</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。给买受人造成损失</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，由出卖人支</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">付</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">【已付房价款一倍</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">】</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">【买受人全部损失】的赔偿</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">金。因此而发生的检测费用由出卖人承担。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买受人不解除合同的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，</span><span style="width: 340.49pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 27.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（二</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">其他质量问题</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房质量应当符合有关工程质量规范、标准和施工图设计文件的要求。发现除地基基础和主体结构外质量问题的，双方按照以下方式处理：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 27.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（ 1）及时更换、修理；如给买受人造成损失的，还应当承担相应赔偿责任。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 423.3pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.65pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">经过更</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">换</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">、修</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">理</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，仍然严重影响正常使用</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，买受人有权解除合</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">同</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。买受人解除合</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">同</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，应当书面通知出卖</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">人</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。出卖人应当自解除合同通知送达之日</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">起</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.75pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">15</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.75pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日内退还买受人已付</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">全部房</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">款</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（含已付贷款部分</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，并自买受人付款之日</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">起</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，按</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">照</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">%</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（不低于中国人民银</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">行公布的同期贷款基准利率</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.85pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">计算给付利息。给买受人造成损失的，由出卖人承担相应赔偿责任。因此而发生的检测费用由出卖人承担。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买受人不解除合同的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，</span><span style="width: 340.49pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 27.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（三</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">装饰装修及设备标准</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65540;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.020.png" width="19" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; margin-left: 452.41pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p></div></div>  
<div><p style="margin-top: 1.2pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房应当使用合格的建筑材料、构配件和设备，装置、装修、装饰所用材料的产品质量必须符合国家的强制性标准及双方约定的标准。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-right: 10.7pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">不符合</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">上</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">述标准</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">受人有权要</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">求</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">出卖人按照</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">下</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">列</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">、</span><span style="width: 109.68pt; text-indent: 0pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">、</span><span style="width: 51.99pt; text-indent: 0pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">方式</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">处理（可多选</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（ 1）及时更换、修理；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（ 2）出卖人赔偿双倍的装饰、设备差价；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">3</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="width: 406.19pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 5.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; text-indent: -5.5pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">4</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="width: 406.19pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。具体装饰装修及相关设备标准的约定见附件六。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（四</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">室内空气质量、建筑隔声和民用建筑节能措施</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房室内空气质量符合【国家</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">】</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">【地方】标准，标准名称</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">：</span><span style="width: 183.73pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 141.25pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，标准文号</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">：</span><span style="width: 92.66pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房为住宅的，建筑隔声情况符合【国家</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">】</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">【地方】标准，标准名称</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">：</span><span style="width: 149.2pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 141.25pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，标准文号</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">：</span><span style="width: 92.66pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-right: 10.55pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房室内空气质量或建筑隔声情况经检测不符合标准，由出卖人负责整改，整改后仍不符合标准的，买受人有权解除合同。买受人解除合同的，应当书面通知出卖人。出卖人应当</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">自解除合同通知送达之日起 15 日内退还买受人已付全部房款</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（含已付贷款部分</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，并自买受人付款之日起，按照</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; letter-spacing: 0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">%（不低于中国人民银行公布的同期贷款基准利率）计算给付利息。给买受人造成损失的，由出卖人承担相应赔偿责任。经检测不符合标准的，检测费用由出卖人承担，整改后再次检测发生的费用仍由出卖人承担。因整改导致该商品房逾期交付的，出卖人应当承担逾期交付责任。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房应当符合国家有关民用建筑节能强制性标准的要求。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">未达到标准的，出卖人应当按照相应标准要求补做节能措施，并承担全部费用；给买受人造成损失的，出卖人应当承担相应赔偿责任。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 423.3pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.15pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第十七条</span><span style="width: 20.78pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">保修责任</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.7pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（一</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.9pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">商品房实行保修制度。该商品房为住宅的，出卖人自该商品房交付之日起，按照《住宅质量保证书》承诺的内容承担相应的保修责任。该商品房为非住宅的，双方应当签订补充协议详细约定保修范围、保修期限和保修责任等内容。具体内容见附件七。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（二</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">下列情形，出卖人不承担保修责任：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">因不可抗力造成的房屋及其附属设施的损害；</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65540;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.021.png" width="19" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; margin-left: 452.41pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p></div></div>  
<div><p style="margin-top: 1.2pt; margin-left: 38.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">因买受人不当使用造成的房屋及其附属设施的损害；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 36.05pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -8.2pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">3.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 415.05pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（三）在保修期内，买受人要求维修的书面通知送达出卖人</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 108.09pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日内，出卖人</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 1.6pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">既不履行保修义务也不提出书面异议的，买受人可以自行或委托他人进行维修，维修费用及维修期间造成的其他损失由出卖人承担。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.95pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第十八条</span><span style="width: 20.78pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">质量担保</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-right: 13.3pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">出卖人不按照第十六条、第十七条约定承担相关责任的，由</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 126.79pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">承担连带责任。关于质量担保的证明见附件八。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 9.05pt; margin-left: 154.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第八章</span><span style="width: 20pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">合同备案与房屋登记</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.65pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 8.5pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第十九条</span><span style="width: 20.78pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">预售合同登记备案</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.4pt; margin-right: 10.45pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（一）出卖人应当自本合同签订之日</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">起</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 1.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">【</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">30</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.3pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日内</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">】</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">【</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 85.86pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日内</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.55pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">】</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（不超</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">过</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">30</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日）办理商</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">品房预售合同登记备案手续，并将本合同登记备案情况告知买受人。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（二</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">有关预售合同登记备案的其他约定如下：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 423.3pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 423.3pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.15pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第二十条</span><span style="width: 20.78pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">房屋登记</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（一</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">双方同意共同向房屋登记机构申请办理该商品房的房屋所有权转移登记。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（二）因出卖人的原因，买受人未能在该商品房交付之日起</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 7.29pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日内取得该商</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 1.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">品房的房屋所有权证书的，双方同意按照下列第</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">种方式处理：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-right: 10.65pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买受人有权解除合同。买受人解除合同的，应当书面通知出卖人。出卖人应当自解除合</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">同通知送达之日</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">起</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">5</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> 日内退还买受人已付全部房</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">款</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（含已付贷款部分</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，并自买受人付款之</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日起，按照</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">%（不低于中国人民银行公布的同期贷款基准利率）计算给付利息。买受人不&nbsp; 解除合同的，自买受人应当完成房屋所有权登记的期限届满之次日起至实际完成房屋所有权登记之日止，出卖人按日计算向买受人支付全部房价款万分之</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">的违约金。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 36.05pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -8.2pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 415.05pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（三</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.2pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">因买受人的原因未能在约定期限内完成该商品房的房屋所有权转移登记的，出卖人不承担责任。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 9.05pt; margin-right: 4.9pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第九章</span><span style="width: 19.95pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">前期物业管理</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.65pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 8.5pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第二十一条</span><span style="width: 23.22pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">前期物业管理</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（一）出卖人依法选聘的前期物业服务企业为</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 257.68pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65540;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.022.png" width="19" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; margin-left: 452.41pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p></div></div>  
<div><p style="margin-top: 1.2pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（二）物业服务时间从</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 65.69pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">年</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 21.69pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">月</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 21.69pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日到</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 46.14pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">年</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 21.69pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">月</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 21.69pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（三）物业服务期</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">间</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，物业收费计费方式</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">为</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">【包干制</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">】</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">【酬金制</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.55pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">】</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">【</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 122.22pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -4.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">】</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。物</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">业</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 1.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">服务费为</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">元 / 月·平方米（建筑面积</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -4.15pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（四）买受人同意由出卖人选聘的前期物业服务企业代为查验并承接物业共用部位、共用设施设备，出卖人应当将物业共用部位、共用设施设备承接查验的备案情况书面告知买受人。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 10.65pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 16.5pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（五）买受人已详细阅读前期物业服务合同和临时管理规约，同意由出卖人依法选聘的物业服务企业实施前期物业管理，遵守临时管理规约。业主委员会成立后，由业主大会决定选聘或续聘物业服务企业。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房前期物业服务合同、临时管理规约见附件九。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.45pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 8.5pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-right: 4.9pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第十章</span><span style="width: 19.95pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">其他事项</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.65pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 8.5pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.05pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第二十二条</span><span style="width: 23.22pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">建筑物区分所有权</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（一</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买受人对其建筑物专有部分享有占有、使用、收益和处分的权利。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（二</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">以下部位归业主共有：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.55pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">建筑物的基础、承重结构、外墙、屋顶等基本结构部分，通道、楼梯、大堂等公共通行部分，消防、公共照明等附属设施、设备，避难层、设备层或者设备间等结构部分；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-right: 10.4pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">该商品房所在建筑区划内的道路</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（属于城镇公共道路的除外</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">、绿地</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（属于城镇公共绿地或者明示属于个人的除外</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">、占用业主共有的道路或者其他场地用于停放汽车的车位、物业</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">服务用房；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 36.05pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -8.2pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">3.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 415.05pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 22.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（三</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">双方对其他配套设施约定如下：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">规划的车位、车库</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">：</span><span style="width: 340.79pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 5.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 132%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;
