letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">会所</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">：</span><span style="width: 392.13pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">； 3.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第二十三条&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 1.75pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">税费</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">双方应当按照国家的有关规定，向相应部门缴纳因该商品房买卖发生的税费。因预测面积与实测面积差异，导致买受人不能享受税收优惠政策而增加的税收负担，由</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 85.25pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">承担。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.15pt; margin-left: 27.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第二十四条</span><span style="width: 23.22pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">销售和使用承诺</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.55pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 5.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.1pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">出卖人承诺不采取分割拆零销售、返本销售或者变相返本销售的方式销售商品房；不采取售后包租或者变相售后包租的方式销售未竣工商品房。</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65540;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.023.png" width="19" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt; margin-left: 452.41pt; position: absolute;"></span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></p></div></div>  
<div><p style="margin-top: 1.2pt; margin-right: 10.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">出卖人承诺按照规划用途进行建设和出售，不擅自改变该商品房使用性质，并按照规划用途办理房屋登记。出卖人不得擅自改变与该商品房有关的共用部位和设施的使用性质。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-right: 10.5pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">3.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">出卖人承诺对商品房的销售，不涉及依法或者依规划属于买受人共有的共用部位和设施的处分。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 43.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">4.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">出卖人承诺已将遮挡或妨碍房屋正常使用的情况告知买受人。具体内容见附件十。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 5.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; line-height: 132%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">5.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买受人使用该商品房期间，不得擅自改变该商品房的用途、建筑主体结构和承重结构。 6.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 78.92pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 9.1pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">7.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第二十五条</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">送达</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-right: 5.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">出卖人和买受人保证在本合同中记载的通讯地址、联系电话均真实有效。任何根据本合同</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">发出的文</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">件</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，均应采用书面形</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">式</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">以</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">【邮政快递</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">】</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">【邮寄挂号信</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -5.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">】</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">【</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">】方式送达对</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">方。任何一方变更通讯地址、联系电话的，应在变更之日起</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">日内书面通知对方。变更的一方 未履行通知义务导致送达不能的，应承担相应的法律责任。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第二十六条</span><span style="width: 23.22pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">买受人信息保护</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.6pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.2pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">出卖人对买受人信息负有保密义务。非因法律、法规规定或国家安全机关、公安机关、检</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.35pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">察机关、审判机关、纪检监察部门执行公务的需要，未经买受人书面同意，出卖人及其销售人员</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">和相关工作人员不得对外披露买受人信息，或将买受人信息用于履行本合同之外的其他用途。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.95pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第二十七条</span><span style="width: 23.22pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">争议解决方式</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">本合同在履行过程中发生的争议，由双方当事人协商解决，也可通过消费者协会等相关机构调解</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.75pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">或按照下列第</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 13.15pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">种方式解决：</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.3pt; margin-left: 43.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">1.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">依法向房屋所在地人民法院起诉。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 43.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-indent: -10.9pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">2.</span><span style="font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">提交</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 125.79pt; text-indent: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">仲裁委员会仲裁。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.15pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第二十八条</span><span style="width: 23.22pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">补充协议</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">对本合同中未约定或约定不明的内容，双方可根据具体情况签订书面补充协议</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 300.05pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -1.7pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -0.25pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">补充协议见附件十一</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 10.75pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 10.85pt; text-indent: 22pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">补充协议中含有不合理的减轻或免除本合同中约定应当由出卖人承担的责任，或不合理的加重买受人责任、排除买受人主要权利内容的，仍以本合同为准。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 0.95pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正黑体_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">第二十九条</span><span style="width: 23.22pt; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">合同生效</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">本合同自双方签字或盖章之日起生效。本合同的解除应当采用书面形式。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 1.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">本合同及附件</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">共</span><span style="width: 59.11pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">份</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: 1.5pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">，其中出卖</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">人</span><span style="width: 59.11pt; letter-spacing: -1.4pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-right: 5.25pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; line-height: 133%; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 423.3pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。6.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 1.25pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">7.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 415.05pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">；</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">8.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);"> </span><span style="width: 415.05pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 27.35pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">（二</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; letter-spacing: -2.8pt; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">）</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">其他约定</span></p><p style="margin-top: 5.45pt; margin-left: 32.85pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-decoration-line: underline; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">&nbsp;</span><span style="width: 423.3pt; font-family: &quot;Lucida Console&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-decoration-line: underline; display: inline-block;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;方正书宋_GBK&quot;; color: rgb(35, 31, 32);">。</span></p><div style=""><p style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; line-height: 6%; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="height: 0pt; display: block; position: absolute; z-index: -65538;"><img src="-qU7L7hl6svJOcq3O.027.png" width="19" height="18" alt="" style="margin-top: -10.46pt;
